subdir=git-gui ; echo '   ' SUBDIR $subdir; make --no-print-directory -C $subdir gitexecdir='/home/richard/libexec/git-core' all
    SUBDIR git-gui
VARS='SHELL_PATH='\''/bin/sh'\'' TCL_PATH='\''tclsh'\'' TCLTK_PATH='\''wish'\'' gitexecdir='\''/home/richard/libexec/git-core'\'' gg_libdir='\''/home/richard/share/git-gui/lib'\'' GITGUI_MACOSXAPP= '; \
if test x"$VARS" != x"`cat GIT-GUI-VARS 2>/dev/null`" ; then \
	echo >&2 "    * new locations or Tcl/Tk interpreter"; \
	echo >GIT-GUI-VARS "$VARS"; \
fi
echo '   ' GEN 'git-gui' &&rm -f git-gui git-gui+ && \
sed -e '1s|#!.*/sh|#!/bin/sh|' \
	-e 's|@@SHELL_PATH@@|/bin/sh|' \
	-e '1,30s|^ argv0=$0| argv0=$0|' \
	-e '1,30s|^ exec wish | exec '\''wish'\'' |' \
	-e 's/@@GITGUI_VERSION@@/0.21.GITGUI-dirty/g' \
	-e 's|@@GITGUI_RELATIVE@@||' \
	-e 's|@@GITGUI_LIBDIR@@|/home/richard/share/git-gui/lib|' \
	git-gui.sh >git-gui+ && \
chmod +x git-gui+ && \
mv git-gui+ git-gui
echo '   ' INDEX lib/ &&if echo \
  source lib/class.tcl\; \
  auto_mkindex lib about.tcl blame.tcl branch.tcl branch_checkout.tcl branch_create.tcl branch_delete.tcl branch_rename.tcl browser.tcl checkout_op.tcl choose_font.tcl choose_repository.tcl choose_rev.tcl class.tcl commit.tcl console.tcl database.tcl date.tcl diff.tcl encoding.tcl error.tcl index.tcl line.tcl logo.tcl merge.tcl mergetool.tcl option.tcl remote.tcl remote_add.tcl remote_branch_delete.tcl search.tcl shortcut.tcl spellcheck.tcl sshkey.tcl status_bar.tcl themed.tcl tools.tcl tools_dlg.tcl transport.tcl win32.tcl \
| tclsh 2>/dev/null; then : ok; \
else \
 echo >&2 "    * tclsh failed; using unoptimized loading"; \
 rm -f lib/tclIndex ; \

subdir=templates ; echo '   ' SUBDIR $subdir; make --no-print-directory -C $subdir SHELL_PATH='/bin/sh' PERL_PATH='/usr/bin/perl'
    SUBDIR templates
umask 022 && ls *--* 2>/dev/null | \
while read boilerplate; \
do \
	case "$boilerplate" in *~) continue ;; esac && \
	dst=`echo "$boilerplate" | sed -e 's|^this|.|;s|--|/|g'` && \
	dir=`expr "$dst" : '\(.*\)/'` && \
	mkdir -p blt/$dir && \
	case "$boilerplate" in \
	*--) continue;; \
	esac && \
	sed -e '1s|#!.*/sh|#!/bin/sh|' \
	    -e 's|@SHELL_PATH@|/bin/sh|' \
	    -e 's|@PERL_PATH@|/usr/bin/perl|g' $boilerplate > \
		blt/$dst && \
	if test -x "$boilerplate"; then rx=rx; else rx=r; fi && \
	chmod a+$rx "blt/$dst" || exit; \
done && \
date >boilerplates.made
